File Under Ska is back!

File Under Ska has been a radio show at the Freies Radio für Stuttgart since June 2003.
We play both kinds - Ska and Rocksteady.

Next shows: 22.09.2023, 20.10.2023, 17.11.2023, 15.12.2023 (Friday, 8 pm till 10 pm)

99,2 MHz in Stuttgart, Livestream: freies-radio.de/player/player.html

Like our Facebook page to stay up to date.

The Homepage until 2017     The WordPress site until 2019

Check out the playlists from 743 shows below.

Upcoming concerts in and around Stuttgart:

  • Fr, 06.10.2023: Rantanplan, Betontod, LKA Longhorn
  • Fr, 13.10.2023: Vintage Trouble, Eberhardstraße 10, Stuttgart
  • Sa, 14.10.2023: The Nite Steadies, Panoptikum Rohr
  • Sa, 14.10.2023: Offbeat Attack mit The Schogettes, Tighten Up, Dynamo Ska, Arte Bellas & The Fellas, DJs: Mrs. Kiki (Frankfurt) und Mr. Blue Beat (Hannover), Nexus Braunschweig
  • Sa, 11.11.2023: The Nite Steadies, Alte Scheune Sindelfingen
  • Sa, 25.11.2023: The Nite Steadies, Waldheim Gaisburg
  • Fr, 23.02.2024: The Busters, Sudhaus Tübingen

Also check out motorcityrock.de, stuttgigs.de and gig-blog.net/calendar
